# Stack Protection Mechanisms in LLVM

## Your Task

Find all C++ source files in `llvm/llvm-project` that implement stack protection mechanisms against buffer overflow attacks. Specifically identify: 1. The LLVM pass that inserts stack protector checks (look for `StackProtector` in `llvm/lib/CodeGen/`). 2. The file that defines the `SafeStack` pass that separates safe and unsafe stack allocations (under `llvm/lib/CodeGen/`). 3. The header file that declares the stack protection pass interface. 4. The compiler-rt runtime file that provides the `__stack_chk_fail` implementation (look under `compiler-rt/lib/builtins/`). 5. Any file in `llvm/lib/Transforms/Instrumentation/` that implements memory safety instrumentation related to stack frame protection. Report the repo, file path, and the primary function or class handling stack protection for each.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the security domain.

## Available Resources

No local repositories are pre-checked out.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `github.com/llvm/llvm-project` (llvm/llvm-project)
- `github.com/gcc-mirror/gcc` (gcc-mirror/gcc)

## Output Format

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:

```json
{
  "files": [
```

## Summary

I've identified **7 key C++ source files** that implement stack protection mechanisms against buffer overflow attacks:

### Main Files Found:

1. **StackProtector Pass** (`llvm/lib/CodeGen/StackProtector.cpp`)
   - Inserts stack protector checks via the `StackProtector` and `StackProtectorPass` classes
   - Core functions: `InsertStackProtectors()`, `CreateFailBB()`

2. **StackProtector Header** (`llvm/include/llvm/CodeGen/StackProtector.h`)
   - Declares pass interfaces and `SSPLayoutInfo`/`SSPLayoutAnalysis` classes

3. **SafeStack Pass** (`llvm/lib/CodeGen/SafeStack.cpp`)
   - Separates stack into safe and unsafe regions
   - Classes: `SafeStack`, `SafeStackPass`, `SafeStackLegacyPass`

4. **SafeStack Header** (`llvm/include/llvm/CodeGen/SafeStack.h`)
   - Declares the `SafeStackPass` interface

5. **Runtime Support** (`libc/src/compiler/generic/__stack_chk_fail.cpp`)
   - Implements `__stack_chk_fail()` function and `__stack_chk_guard` global variable
   - Called when canary corruption is detected

6. **AddressSanitizer** (`llvm/lib/Transforms/Instrumentation/AddressSanitizer.cpp`)
   - Memory safety instrumentation with `FunctionStackPoisoner` class

7. **HWAddressSanitizer** (`llvm/lib/Transforms/Instrumentation/HWAddressSanitizer.cpp`)
   - Hardware-assisted memory tagging for stack protection

The output file includes complete metadata about files, symbols, and a comprehensive narrative explaining LLVM's defense-in-depth strategy against stack-based attacks.

Mechanisms in LLVM\\n\\nThis analysis identifies the key C++ source files and classes in the LLVM project that implement stack protection mechanisms against buffer overflow attacks:\\n\\n### 1. StackProtector Pass (llvm/lib/CodeGen/)\\nThe **StackProtector** pass is the primary mechanism for inserting stack protector checks. Located in `llvm/lib/CodeGen/StackProtector.cpp`, this pass implements:\\n- **StackProtector class**: A FunctionPass that inserts stack protectors into functions that need them\\n- **StackProtectorPass class**: The new-style PassInfoMixin for integration with the new pass manager\\n- **SSPLayoutInfo class**: Manages the stack protector layout information\\n- **SSPLayoutAnalysis class**: Analyzes which functions require stack protection\\n\\nThe pass stores a canary value (stack guard) onto the stack before local variables are allocated and checks it upon function exit via the `__stack_chk_fail()` function.\\n\\n### 2. SafeStack Pass (llvm/lib/CodeGen/)\\nThe **SafeStack** pass separates the stack into safe and unsafe regions. Defined in `llvm/lib/CodeGen/SafeStack.cpp`, it includes:\\n- **SafeStack class**: The core implementation that splits stack allocations\\n- **SafeStackPass class**: New-style pass interface (PassInfoMixin)\\n- **SafeStackLegacyPass class**: Legacy pass interface (FunctionPass)\\n- **SafeStackLayout class**: (in SafeStackLayout.h) manages layout of unsafe stack objects\\n\\nThis pass is instrumental in defending against stack-based buffer overflows by explicitly allocating unsafe stack objects in a separate memory region managed through the runtime library.\\n\\n### 3. Stack Protection Header Files\\n- **llvm/include/llvm/CodeGen/StackProtector.h**: Declares the StackProtector pass interface, including SSPLayoutInfo and SSPLayoutAnalysis\\n- **llvm/include/llvm/CodeGen/SafeStack.h**: Declares the SafeStackPass interface\\n\\n### 4. Runtime Support: __stack_chk_fail (compiler-rt/libc)\\nThe **__stack_chk_fail** function is the runtime implementation called when stack corruption is detected. Located in `libc/src/compiler/generic/__stack_chk_fail.cpp`, it:\\n- Declares and defines the `__stack_chk_guard` global variable (initialized with a random canary value)\\n- Implements `__stack_chk_fail()`: Prints \\\"stack smashing detected\\\" and calls abort() when the canary is corrupted\\n\\n### 5. Memory Safety Instrumentation in llvm/lib/Transforms/Instrumentation/\\nTwo additional files provide memory safety instrumentation related to stack frame protection:\\n- **AddressSanitizer.cpp**: Contains the **FunctionStackPoisoner** class that poisons stack memory on function entry and unpoisons on exit, detecting use-after-return and stack overflow violations\\n- **HWAddressSanitizer.cpp**: Implements the **HWAddressSanitizer** class with hardware-assisted memory tagging for stack instrumentation\\n\\nThese instrumentation passes complement the traditional stack protector by detecting broader classes of memory safety violations beyond simple buffer overflows.\\n\\n### Key Functions and Classes Summary\\n\\n**Stack Protection Core:**\\n- `StackProtector::runOnFunction()` - Main entry point for the legacy StackProtector pass\\n- `StackProtectorPass::run()` - Entry point for the new-style pass\\n- `InsertStackProtectors()` - Inserts prologue/epilogue checks\\n- `CreateFailBB()` - Creates the failure block that calls `__stack_chk_fail()`\\n\\n**SafeStack:**\\n- `SafeStackPass::run()` - New-style pass entry point\\n- `SafeStackLegacyPass::runOnFunction()` - Legacy pass entry point\\n- `SafeStack::run()` - Core implementation of stack splitting\\n\\n**Runtime:**\\n- `__stack_chk_fail()` - Runtime handler for corrupted canary detection\\n- `__stack_chk_guard` - Global canary value\\n\\n**Memory Safety Instrumentation:**\\n- `FunctionStackPoisoner` - Instruments stack allocations with shadow memory\\n- `HWAddressSanitizer::instrumentStack()` - Hardware-based memory tagging\\n\\nAll files are part of the LLVM project's comprehensive defense-in-depth strategy against stack-based attacks and memory corruption vulnerabilities.\"\n}\n",

Located in `llvm/lib/CodeGen/StackProtector.cpp`, this pass implements:\\n- **StackProtector class**: A FunctionPass that inserts stack protectors into functions that need them\\n- **StackProtectorPass class**: The new-style PassInfoMixin for integration with the new pass manager\\n- **SSPLayoutInfo class**: Manages the stack protector layout information\\n- **SSPLayoutAnalysis class**: Analyzes which functions require stack protection\\n\\nThe pass stores a canary value (stack guard) onto the stack before local variables are allocated and checks it upon function exit via the `__stack_chk_fail()` function.\\n\\n### 2. SafeStack Pass (llvm/lib/CodeGen/)\\nThe **SafeStack** pass separates the stack into safe and unsafe regions. Defined in `llvm/lib/CodeGen/SafeStack.cpp`, it includes:\\n- **SafeStack class**: The core implementation that splits stack allocations\\n- **SafeStackPass class**: New-style pass interface (PassInfoMixin)\\n- **SafeStackLegacyPass class**: Legacy pass interface (FunctionPass)\\n- **SafeStackLayout class**: (in SafeStackLayout.h) manages layout of unsafe stack objects\\n\\nThis pass is instrumental in defending against stack-based buffer overflows by explicitly allocating unsafe stack objects in a separate memory region managed through the runtime library.\\n\\n### 3. Stack Protection Header Files\\n- **llvm/include/llvm/CodeGen/StackProtector.h**: Declares the StackProtector pass interface, including SSPLayoutInfo and SSPLayoutAnalysis\\n- **llvm/include/llvm/CodeGen/SafeStack.h**: Declares the SafeStackPass interface\\n\\n### 4. Runtime Support: __stack_chk_fail (compiler-rt/libc)\\nThe **__stack_chk_fail** function is the runtime implementation called when stack corruption is detected. Located in `libc/src/compiler/generic/__stack_chk_fail.cpp`, it:\\n- Declares and defines the `__stack_chk_guard` global variable (initialized with a random canary value)\\n- Implements `__stack_chk_fail()`: Prints \\\"stack smashing detected\\\" and calls abort() when the canary is corrupted\\n\\n### 5. Memory Safety Instrumentation in llvm/lib/Transforms/Instrumentation/\\nTwo additional files provide memory safety instrumentation related to stack frame protection:\\n- **AddressSanitizer.cpp**: Contains the **FunctionStackPoisoner** class that poisons stack memory on function entry and unpoisons on exit, detecting use-after-return and stack overflow violations\\n- **HWAddressSanitizer.cpp**: Implements the **HWAddressSanitizer** class with hardware-assisted memory tagging for stack instrumentation\\n\\nThese instrumentation passes complement the traditional stack protector by detecting broader classes of memory safety violations beyond simple buffer overflows.\\n\\n### Key Functions and Classes Summary\\n\\n**Stack Protection Core:**\\n- `StackProtector::runOnFunction()` - Main entry point for the legacy StackProtector pass\\n- `StackProtectorPass::run()` - Entry point for the new-style pass\\n- `InsertStackProtectors()` - Inserts prologue/epilogue checks\\n- `CreateFailBB()` - Creates the failure block that calls `__stack_chk_fail()`\\n\\n**SafeStack:**\\n- `SafeStackPass::run()` - New-style pass entry point\\n- `SafeStackLegacyPass::runOnFunction()` - Legacy pass entry point\\n- `SafeStack::run()` - Core implementation of stack splitting\\n\\n**Runtime:**\\n- `__stack_chk_fail()` - Runtime handler for corrupted canary detection\\n- `__stack_chk_guard` - Global canary value\\n\\n**Memory Safety Instrumentation:**\\n- `FunctionStackPoisoner` - Instruments stack allocations with shadow memory\\n- `HWAddressSanitizer::instrumentStack()` - Hardware-based memory tagging\\n\\nAll files are part of the LLVM project's comprehensive defense-in-depth strategy against stack-based attacks and memory corruption vulnerabilities.\"\n}\n",
